tors, xelSekruleba ki daido imave wlis 31 agvistos, e.i. S.CilaCava

SemTxvevaSi, warmodgenili piri _ Sps `saqwigni~ Tanaxma rom iyo xel-

bis SemTxvevaSi. e.i. mas Semdeg, rac Sps-m yofili direqtoris S.Cali-

debis momentidan da igi (Sps) valdebuli aris am garigebiT nakisri


valdebulebani Seasrulos (gadaixados saijaro qira, gaaTavisuflos


farTi saijaro xelSekrulebis Sewyvetis Semdeg da a.S.)

ze, dausabuTebelia.

da 250 laris dabruneba.

raSvilis warmomadgenelma, romelic moiTxovs gasaCivrebuli ganCi-


nebis gauqmebas da saqmis xelaxla gansaxilvelad dabrunebas.

sk-is 183-e muxli, vinaidan mosarCele moiTxovda kuTvnili nivTis


(Tanxis) dabrunebas an Secvlas sxva nivTiT. kanonier ZalaSi Sesuli


gadawyvetilebiT dadgenilia, rom mxareTa SeTanxmebis safuZvelze


moxda ori nivTis (binisa da Tanxis) droebiTi gacvla. v. ficxelaur-


ma ver daabruna Tanxa da igi sadavo binas flobs dRemde.

gadascems ficxelauris binas.

safuZvlebi da Tvlis, rom sakasacio saCivari ar unda dakmayofil-

ze, romlis safuZvelzec sasamarTlos igi unda ecno sadavo binis me-


sakuTred.

Zenad aucilebelia sanotaro wesiT damowmebuli sabuTi da SemZenis


registracia sajaro reestrSi.


dadgenilia, rom mosarCeles sadavo binaze sakuTrebis SeZenis ra-


ime damadasturebeli sabuTi ar warmoudgenia. bina ekuTvnoda v. fic-


xelaurs, romelic gardaicvala 2001 wels.

sxvaveba ganpirobebulia moZrav da uZrav nivTebze sakuTrebis war-


moSobis gansxvavebuli reJimiT. Tu moZravi nivTebis SeZenisaTvis
